# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# etcd Raft Snapshot Too Old on Node Rejoin

## Your Task

An etcd node fails to rejoin a cluster with 'ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable'. Find the Go source files in etcd-io/etcd that (1) define ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable and (2) implement the snapshot availability check during Raft log catch-up.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the incident domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
*(none — all repos available locally)*


## Summary

**ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable** is defined in the `github.com/etcd-io/raft` module (part of the `go.etcd.io/raft/v3` dependency used by etcd). The error defines the behavior when an etcd node fails to rejoin a cluster during Raft log catch-up.

### Key Files:

1. **raft/storage.go (line 38)** - Defines `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` as a sentinel error returned when the Storage interface's `Snapshot()` method indicates the snapshot is not yet ready.

2. **raft/log.go** - Contains the `snapshot()` method that retrieves snapshots, checking unstable snapshots first before delegating to the storage backend.

3. **raft/raft.go** - Contains the `maybeSendAppend()` function (lines ~469-474) where the availability check occurs. When a rejoining node is too far behind, the leader attempts snapshot transfer. If `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` is returned, the function gracefully returns false without sending a message, allowing retry on the next Raft tick.

4. **raft/tracker/progress.go** - Manages follower progress state transitions, including `BecomeSnapshot()` which updates progress when snapshot transfer begins.

5. **raft/tracker/state.go** - Manages the `StateSnapshot` state, which pauses all replication until snapshot transfer completes.

The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json` with complete details about the files, symbols, and the call chain involved in handling snapshot availability during node rejoin scenarios.

Here's a comprehensive breakdown:\\n\\n---\\n\\n## `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` \u2014 Definition and Usage\\n\\n### 1. Definition\\n\\n`ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` is defined in [`raft/storage.go` (line 38)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/storage.go?L36-38):\\n\\n```go\\n// ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable is returned by the Storage interface when the required\\n// snapshot is temporarily unavailable.\\nvar ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable = errors.New(\\\"snapshot is temporarily unavailable\\\")\\n```\\n\\nIt is specified as part of the `Storage` interface contract on the [`Snapshot()` method (lines 67\u201371)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/storage.go?L67-71):\\n\\n```go\\n// Snapshot returns the most recent snapshot.\\n// If snapshot is temporarily unavailable, it should return ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable,\\n// so raft state machine could know that Storage needs some time to prepare\\n// snapshot and call Snapshot later.\\nSnapshot() (pb.Snapshot, error)\\n```\\n\\nThis is a **signal contract**: custom `Storage` implementations (e.g., those with async or disk-backed snapshot generation) return this to tell the Raft state machine \\\"not yet, try again later.\\\" The built-in [`MemoryStorage.Snapshot()`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/storage.go?L165-170) never returns this error \u2014 it's always immediately available.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### 2. Here's the full flow:\\n\\n#### Step 1 \u2014 Try to send log entries\\nThe leader looks up the follower's [`Progress`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/tracker/progress.go?L30-80) tracker and tries to retrieve the entries from its next expected index (`pr.Next`):\\n\\n```go\\nterm, errt := r.raftLog.term(pr.Next - The Raft heartbeat/tick cycle will cause `maybeSendAppend()` to be called again on the next tick, retrying the snapshot.\\n- **Any other error**: panics immediately (unrecoverable).\\n\\n#### Step 4 \u2014 Snapshot is sent and follower transitions to `StateSnapshot`\\n\\nIf the snapshot is available, the leader sends a `MsgSnap` message and transitions the follower's progress via [`pr.BecomeSnapshot(sindex)` (line 483)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/raft.go?L483):\\n\\n```go\\nm.Snapshot = snapshot\\npr.BecomeSnapshot(sindex)  // sets pr.State = StateSnapshot, pr.PendingSnapshot = sindex\\n```\\n\\nWhile in [`StateSnapshot`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/tracker/state.go?L32-33), `IsPaused()` unconditionally returns `true` \u2014 the leader halts all further replication to that peer until the snapshot completes:\\n\\n```go\\ncase StateSnapshot:\\n    return true  // always paused\\n```\\n\\n#### Step 5 \u2014 Follower acknowledges and resumes replication\\n\\nOn the follower side, [`handleSnapshot()` in `raft/raft.go`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/raft.go?L1393-1404) applies the snapshot via `restore()`, then sends a `MsgAppResp` back to the leader. Here's a comprehensive breakdown:\n\n---\n\n## `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` \u2014 Definition and Usage\n\n### 1. Definition\n\n`ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` is defined in [`raft/storage.go` (line 38)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/storage.go?L36-38):\n\n```go\n// ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable is returned by the Storage interface when the required\n// snapshot is temporarily unavailable.\nvar ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable = errors.New(\"snapshot is temporarily unavailable\")\n```\n\nIt is specified as part of the `Storage` interface contract on the [`Snapshot()` method (lines 67\u201371)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/storage.go?L67-71):\n\n```go\n// Snapshot returns the most recent snapshot.\n// If snapshot is temporarily unavailable, it should return ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable,\n// so raft state machine could know that Storage needs some time to prepare\n// snapshot and call Snapshot later.\nSnapshot() (pb.Snapshot, error)\n```\n\nThis is a **signal contract**: custom `Storage` implementations (e.g., those with async or disk-backed snapshot generation) return this to tell the Raft state machine \"not yet, try again later.\" The built-in [`MemoryStorage.Snapshot()`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/storage.go?L165-170) never returns this error \u2014 it's always immediately available.\n\n---\n\n### 2. How Snapshot Availability Is Checked During Log Catch-Up\n\nWhen a **lagging node rejoins** the cluster and needs to catch up, the leader handles it via [`maybeSendAppend()` in `raft/raft.go` (lines 447\u2013506)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/raft.go?L447-506). Here's the full flow:\n\n#### Step 1 \u2014 Try to send log entries\nThe leader looks up the follower's [`Progress`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/tracker/progress.go?L30-80) tracker and tries to retrieve the entries from its next expected index (`pr.Next`):\n\n```go\nterm, errt := r.raftLog.term(pr.Next - 1)\nents, erre := r.raftLog.entries(pr.Next, r.maxMsgSize)\n```\n\n#### Step 2 \u2014 Fall back to snapshot if entries are unavailable\nIf `errt != nil || erre != nil` (i.e., the required entries have been compacted away \u2014 the node is too far behind), the leader falls back to sending a full snapshot:\n\n```go\nif errt != nil || erre != nil { // send snapshot if we failed to get term or entries\n    if !pr.RecentActive {\n        // Ignore \u2014 follower hasn't been heard from recently\n        return false\n    }\n\n    m.Type = pb.MsgSnap\n    snapshot, err := r.raftLog.snapshot()  // calls l.storage.Snapshot()\n```\n\n#### Step 3 \u2014 Snapshot availability check\n\n[`raftLog.snapshot()`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/log.go?L170-175) first checks for an in-memory unstable snapshot, then delegates to the application's `Storage`:\n\n```go\nfunc (l *raftLog) snapshot() (pb.Snapshot, error) {\n    if l.unstable.snapshot != nil {\n        return *l.unstable.snapshot, nil\n    }\n    return l.storage.Snapshot()\n}\n```\n\nBack in `maybeSendAppend()`, **this is where `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` is caught** [(lines 469\u2013474)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/raft.go?L469-474):\n\n```go\nif err != nil {\n    if err == ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable {\n        r.logger.Debugf(\"%x failed to send snapshot to %x because snapshot is temporarily unavailable\", r.id, to)\n        return false  // \u2190 silently bail; will retry on next tick\n    }\n    panic(err) // any other error is fatal\n}\n```\n\n- **If `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable`**: returns `false` \u2014 no message is sent this tick. The Raft heartbeat/tick cycle will cause `maybeSendAppend()` to be called again on the next tick, retrying the snapshot.\n- **Any other error**: panics immediately (unrecoverable).\n\n#### Step 4 \u2014 Snapshot is sent and follower transitions to `StateSnapshot`\n\nIf the snapshot is available, the leader sends a `MsgSnap` message and transitions the follower's progress via [`pr.BecomeSnapshot(sindex)` (line 483)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/raft.go?L483):\n\n```go\nm.Snapshot = snapshot\npr.BecomeSnapshot(sindex)  // sets pr.State = StateSnapshot, pr.PendingSnapshot = sindex\n```\n\nWhile in [`StateSnapshot`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/tracker/state.go?L32-33), `IsPaused()` unconditionally returns `true` \u2014 the leader halts all further replication to that peer until the snapshot completes:\n\n```go\ncase StateSnapshot:\n    return true  // always paused\n```\n\n#### Step 5 \u2014 Follower acknowledges and resumes replication\n\nOn the follower side, [`handleSnapshot()` in `raft/raft.go`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/raft.go?L1393-1404) applies the snapshot via `restore()`, then sends a `MsgAppResp` back to the leader. The leader uses this to transition the follower back to `StateProbe` \u2192 `StateReplicate` and resume normal log replication.\n\n---\n\n### Summary\n\n| Component | File | Role |\n|---|---|---|\n| The error signals that the Raft state machine should retry later.\\n\\nDuring node rejoin for log catch-up, the snapshot availability check follows this chain:\\n\\n1. **Definition (raft/storage.go:38)**: ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable is defined as part of the Storage interface contract for the Snapshot() method. Custom Storage implementations (e.g., with async snapshot generation) return this error to indicate the snapshot is not yet ready.\\n\\n2. **Snapshot Retrieval (raft/log.go)**: The raftLog.snapshot() method checks for unstable snapshots first, then delegates to storage.Snapshot(). This is called when the leader needs to send a snapshot to a lagging follower.\\n\\n3. **Availability Check During Log Catch-Up (raft/raft.go - maybeSendAppend() function, lines ~469-474)**: When a rejoining node is too far behind and required log entries are compacted away, the leader attempts to send a snapshot. If storage.Snapshot() returns ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable, the leader logs a debug message and returns false without sending a message. This silently bails out, and the Raft heartbeat/tick cycle will retry on the next tick.\\n\\n4. **Progress State Management (raft/tracker/progress.go)**: When a snapshot is successfully retrieved and sent, the follower's progress transitions via BecomeSnapshot(sindex), setting the state to StateSnapshot.\\n\\n5. **Pausing Replication (raft/tracker/state.go)**: While in StateSnapshot, IsPaused() returns true, halting all further replication to that peer until the snapshot transfer completes.\\n\\nThe flow handles the specific scenario: when an etcd node fails to rejoin a cluster with 'ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable', it means the cluster leader attempted to catch the rejoining node up via snapshot, but the snapshot was not immediately available. The Raft protocol gracefully handles this by retrying on subsequent ticks until the snapshot becomes available.\"\n}\n",
